LLC vs. S Corp vs. C Corp vs.

Nonprofit — Let’s Break It Down

Choosing your business structure is a big deal, but it doesn’t have to be a big mystery. We’re here to make it clear, founder-focused, and forward-moving.

[Compare Business Types Compare Business Types](https://bizee.com/business-formation/business-entity-comparison)

Got Questions? We've Got Answers.


-------------------------------------

*   1
    
    What’s the difference between an LLC and Corporation?
    
    **LLC vs. Corporation at a glance:  
    LLC (Limited Liability Company)**
    
    *   Offers limited liability protection—your personal assets are shielded from business liabilities.
    *   Simple structure and ideal for small teams or solo founders.
    *   Pass-through taxation: profits and losses flow through to your personal tax return.
    *   Minimal formalities—no annual meetings or boards required.
    
    **Corporation (C‑Corp / S‑Corp)**
    
    *   Also provides limited liability.
    *   C‑Corp: subject to double taxation (corporate profits + shareholder dividends), more formal structure, can issue multiple stock classes—great for scaling and raising capital.
    *   S‑Corp: avoids double-tax with pass-through earnings, more compliance (max 100 shareholders, one stock type).
    
    **In short:** choose an LLC if you’re launching a small, flexible business. Choose a corporation if you're planning to raise investment and grow big.
    
*   2
    
    How long does it take to form a business?
    
    Timeframe varies by state: filing can take a few days to several weeks. Bizee can expedite the process with next-business-day paperwork filing.
    
*   3
    
    Is it really free to form an LLC with Bizee?
    
    Yes—Bizee's Basic package is $0 plus state filing fees. Bizee covers all service costs; you only pay what your state requires. No hidden fees, no surprise add-ons.
    
*   4
    
    What state should I form my business in?
    
    Most entrepreneurs choose to form in their **home state**, where they mainly operate. That's the simplest, avoids foreign qualification. However, some choose states like **Delaware** due to its business-friendly laws (for larger or investment-seeking companies). Bizee offers [state‑by‑state guides](https://bizee.com/llc-formation-by-state)
     to help you decide.

How to Form a S Corporation with Bizee in 3 Simple Steps


------------------------------------------------------------

  ![How To Form A S Corp Info 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZvcm0tYS1zLWNvcnAtaW5mby0xLndlYnA/how-to-form-a-s-corp-info-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

01

Choose Your Incorporation State

Rules and regulations vary by state, so make sure you know the state in which you want your business to be located. You don’t have to choose the state you live in.

  ![Choose The Package Premium](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvY2hvb3NlLXRoZS1wYWNrYWdlLXByZW1pdW0ud2VicA/choose-the-package-premium.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

02

Choose the Package

Whether you only need the basics or want more extensive business support, Bizee has the ideal business formation package to help you start and grow your corporation.

  ![Tell Us About Your S Corp](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvdGVsbC11cy1hYm91dC15b3VyLXMtY29ycC53ZWJw/tell-us-about-your-s-corp.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

03

Tell Us About Your S Corporation

Complete an online order form with the details of your S Corp. You’ll need to supply information about the number of directors and information relating to stock, including the value of shares and number of shareholders.

Common Questions About Starting an S Corporation


----------------------------------------------------

*   1
    
    Can I Start an S Corp for free?
    
    Yes! With our $0 S Corp formation package, you only pay the fees required by your state. Bizee's filing services are free.
    
*   2
    
    How Much Does Your Service Cost?
    
    Since 2004 we’ve been improving and perfecting our service. Streamlined processes keep our costs down so we can pass the savings back to you. The result is a low-cost yet personalized business formation with fast and friendly service.
    
    The Basic package costs $0 + state fee and includes the fundamentals needed to start an S Corp.
    
    The Standard package is $199 + state fee. It’s the option most clients choose due to its comprehensive feature set to get your business started. Your EIN Business Tax number is included (while most other incorporation services charge extra fees on top of their equivalent package price for this). Our Standard package also includes IRS Form 2553, corporation bylaws, operating agreement, banking resolution, lifetime company alerts, online dashboard access, unlimited phone and email support, a business banking account and a business tax consultation.
    
    The Premium package is our best value package at $299 + state fee and offers a full suite of features. Premium includes all of the Standard benefits plus business contract templates, expedited filing and a domain name and business email.
    
    When you form your S Corp with us, our Registered Agent service is free for the first year and is only $119 per year after that.
    
    For more information on our services and prices, visit our [how it works](https://bizee.com/how-it-works)
     page.
    
*   3
    
    Are There Specific Rules For My State?
    
    Each state has specific rules and requirements regarding Registered Agents, naming rules, business licenses, etc. Find out more about S Corps in your state and review our [business entity comparison](https://bizee.com/form/business-entity-comparison)
     chart to learn about liability protection, business fees and tax.
    
*   4
    
    What’s My State’s Filing Fee for S Corps?
    
    Filing costs to form an S Corp can vary from state to state. Use our [free filing fees](https://bizee.com/state-filing-fees)
     chart to easily compare state fees before you start your business.
    

  ![Man With Laptop Desktop](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvcmFuZG9tLWN0YS1iYW5uZXJzL21hbi13aXRoLWxhcHRvcC1kZXNrdG9wLndlYnA/man-with-laptop-desktop.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Key Questions and Answers

A Comprehensive Guide for Startups
----------------------------------

  ![business-formation-officially-registered](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtZm9ybWF0aW9uLW9mZmljaWFsbHktcmVnaXN0ZXJlZC53ZWJw/business-formation-officially-registered.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

  ![business-formation-officially-registered-copy](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtZm9ybWF0aW9uLW9mZmljaWFsbHktcmVnaXN0ZXJlZC1jb3B5LndlYnA/business-formation-officially-registered-copy.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

1.

### What Is an LLC?

  ![business-formation-officially-registered](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtZm9ybWF0aW9uLW9mZmljaWFsbHktcmVnaXN0ZXJlZC53ZWJw/business-formation-officially-registered.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

2.

### Is Starting an LLC Right for You?

  ![business-formation-officially-registered-copy](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtZm9ybWF0aW9uLW9mZmljaWFsbHktcmVnaXN0ZXJlZC1jb3B5LndlYnA/business-formation-officially-registered-copy.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Form My LLC


---------------

Entrepreneurship is booming, and we're proud to be one of America's fastest-growing companies. Here's how you can start your LLC in six straightforward steps:

*   1
    
    ### Name Your LLC
    
    Your business name is the first impression you make. It's essential to pick a name that stands out and accurately represents your brand. In addition to selecting a unique name, you'll need to include a designator like "LLC" or "Limited Company" to indicate your business structure.  
      
    Tips:  
      
    
    *   Use our [Business Name Search](https://bizee.com/business-formation/business-name-search)
         tool to check the availability in your state.
    *   **Not settled on a business name yet, our [Name Generator](https://bizee.com/resources/business-name-generator)
         can help.**
    
*   2
    
    ### Provide an Address
    
    Your LLC needs an official business address. This could be your home address if you're running a home-based business, a rented office space, or even a [virtual address](https://bizee.com/business-management/virtual-mailbox)
    . Remember to check your state's regulations, as some states do not accept P.O. Box addresses.  
      
    Pro Tip:  
      
    A Virtual Address can provide privacy and the flexibility to manage your mail from anywhere. Check out our [Virtual Address Service](https://bizee.com/business-management/virtual-mailbox)
     for a reliable solution.
    
*   3
    
    ### Assign a Registered Agent
    
    A Registered Agent receives official state correspondence on behalf of the company and must be physically available during business hours. While you can act as your own registered agent, we recommend using a [professional service](https://bizee.com/business-management/registered-agent)
     to avoid the hassle and maintain privacy.  
      
    Why Choose Us?  
      
    With any of our business formation packages, you get one year of Registered Agent Service for free. Let us handle the details so you can focus on growing your business.
    
*   4
    
    ### Provide Names and Addresses of LLC Members
    
    You'll need to submit the names and addresses of all your LLC members to the state. This step is straightforward but crucial for maintaining transparency and compliance.  
      
    Note: You can use street addresses or P.O. boxes for your LLC members' addresses, depending on your state's requirements.
    
*   5
    
    ### State the Purpose of Your LLC
    
    When filing your LLC, you must state the purpose of your business. This can be a specific description or a broad statement like "any lawful purpose." If you're still refining your business idea, a general statement will suffice and gives you the flexibility to expand later.  
      
    **Quick Tip:**  
      
    Keeping it simple with "any lawful purpose" covers most business activities  
    and can save time during the filing process.
    
*   6
    
    ### File the Articles of Organization
    
    The final step is to file your Articles of Organization with the state and pay the associated fees. This document officially creates your LLC. Filing can be done online or by mail, depending on your state.  
      
    **Quick Tip:**  
      
    Bizee handles all the paperwork and filing for you, ensuring everything is done correctly and efficiently. Save time and reduce stress by letting us take care of this crucial step.

Benefits of an LLC
------------------

Every savvy entrepreneur knows that weighing the pros and cons is essential. Let’s dive into why an LLC could be your startup’s best friend.

![Check Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus.svg)

### Pros

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### Limited Liability Protection

Even more than limited liability partnerships, LLCs offer some of the strongest available protections for your members’ personal assets.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### Pass-Through Taxation

Simplify taxes by merging your business income with your personal income.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### Flexible Management

Operate your business how you see fit, whether as a member-managed or manager-managed LLC.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### No Ownership Restrictions

Partner with anyone, including foreign nationals.  
Add as many members to the LLC as you need.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### Minimal Compliance

Enjoy fewer regulations compared to corporations. Many LLCs simply need a registered agent and to file an annual report.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/plus-circle.svg)

#### Versatile Tax Status

Opt to be taxed as a sole proprietor/partnership or as an S Corp to benefit your business.

![Check Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/minus.svg)

### Cons

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/minus-circle.svg)

#### Franchise Taxes

Some states impose income-based or flat-fee taxes on all businesses other than sole proprietors.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/minus-circle.svg)

#### Strict Record-Keeping

Maintaining clear separation between personal and business finances will increase your bookkeeping needs.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/minus-circle.svg)

#### Investor Restrictions

While LLCs allow for an unlimited number of members, there are some restrictions on the allowable types of investments.

![List Item Icon](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/minus-circle.svg)

#### Lacks Partnership Structure

Some professionals like lawyers and accountants prefer the rigid, collaborative nature of limited partnerships.

Frequently Asked Questions


------------------------------

*   1
    
    ### Do I need to form an LLC to start a business?
    
    If you begin operating as a business by yourself or with someone else you will be considered a sole proprietor or a partnership unless you specifically file for an LLC. However this can leave your personal assets vulnerable and for that reason we recommend forming an LLC. Learn how to convert your sole proprietorship into an LLC.
    
*   2
    
    ### What does it cost to own an LLC?
    
    The only cost to form an LLC is the state filing fee, but there are often compliance costs to staying in good standing with your state. Unless serving as your own agent, you must maintain a Registered Agent Service for your LLC. This applies to newly formed LLCs too, but with Bizee, new LLCs get one free year of Registered Agent Service. Submitting an Annual Report is the other common cost of owning an LLC. Aside from a handful of states who do not require a filing fee, this may cost anywhere from $10-$500.   
      
    Some states have no income tax, but most have at least a personal income tax that applies to pass-through income. A few states also levy franchise taxes on LLCs regardless of whether the company generates income. All-in-all, the annual cost to own an LLC is usually **at least $100 but rarely over $1,000** (not counting federal and state tax liabilities).
    
*   3
    
    ### Is an LLC a corporation?
    
    No, Limited Liability Companies have a distinct business structure and legal status from corporations on both the state and federal level. There are numerous practical differences, but the main statutory difference is that LLCs cannot sell company shares or stocks and are thus limited in how they raise investment capital. Notably, however, an LLC does have the same limited liability responsibilities as a corporation.
    
*   4
    
    ### How do I file an amendment for an LLC?
    
    If you need to make a change to your LLC, you'll need to file an Amendment by contacting your Secretary of State. Not all changes need to be amended, but generally, any changes to your Articles of Organization will need to be filed. [File Articles of Amendment](https://bizee.com/business-management/articles-of-amendment)
     with Bizee.
    
*   5
    
    ### How do LLC taxes work?
    
    LLCs can be taxed differently depending on whether they are single member or have multiple members, and whether or not you elect to be taxed as a corporation. You can speak with your accountant for more information. Learn more about [LLC taxes](https://bizee.com/articles/business-management/federal-taxes-for-llcs)
     and [smart financial planning](https://bizee.com/financial-planning)
     for your business.
    

![Verified Duocolor](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/verified_duocolor.svg)

Importance of a Great Business Name
-----------------------------------

Your business name significantly impacts how customers perceive your brand. A short, fitting, and distinctive name demonstrates confidence, defines your business, and generates buzz. It is the foundation for your entire brand.

   ![Man Working Outside With A Laptop 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbWFuLXdvcmtpbmctb3V0c2lkZS13aXRoLWEtbGFwdG9wLTEud2VicA/man-working-outside-with-a-laptop-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Man Working Outside With A Laptop 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbWFuLXdvcmtpbmctb3V0c2lkZS13aXRoLWEtbGFwdG9wLTEud2VicA/man-working-outside-with-a-laptop-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

FAQs


--------

*   1
    
    Do I Need to Have a Distinctive Name for My Business?
    
    A distinctive business name helps your brand stand out, enhances recognition, and minimizes the risk of legal conflicts with similar names in your industry.
    
*   2
    
    Are There Rules on What Makes a Business Name Unique?
    
    Yes, there are guidelines for creating a unique business name:
    
    *   It should not be too similar to existing business names.
    *   Avoid using common industry terms.
    *   It must not infringe on trademarks.
    *   Follow specific naming rules for your state or country.
    *   Ensure the name stands out to prevent customer confusion.
    
*   3
    
    How Do I Lookup My Proposed LLC or Corporation Business Name?
    
    It's easy: just use the Business Name Search Tool and enter your proposed LLC or corporation name. We'll search the business name registry for your desired state and tell you if there are any matches. If not, good news — you can form a business with that name, and [we'll help you get started](https://orders.bizee.com/form-order-now.php)
    .
    
*   4
    
    What Happens If I Don't Want to Do Business Under My Legal Entity Name?
    
    Most states allow you to conduct business under a different name. Depending on your state's rules, this could be known as an "assumed name", "fictitious name", "doing business as name" or "trade name". We can file your [Fictitious Business Name](https://bizee.com/file-dba)
     with your state on your behalf.
    
*   5
    
    How Can I Change My Legal Business Name?
    
    You can file an amendment to your Articles of Incorporation or Articles of Organization with your state. We can take care of this and [file the amendment on your behalf](https://bizee.com/form/manage-your-company/amendment)
     to change the name of your LLC or corporation.
    
*   6
    
    Can I Protect the Name of My LLC or Corporation?
    
    Once you have filed and formed your business legally, nobody else can form a business with the same name in that state. If you want extra protection, you could consider [registering your business name as a trademark](https://bizee.com/business-formation/trademark-registration)
    . Note that filing a fictitious or "doing business as" (DBA) name will not be sufficient to protect your business name.
    

### 

We’ll Take Care  
of the Entity Search

We will tell you if your business name is available in your state.

File a DBA or Fictitious Business Name


==========================================

Doing business under a name other than your own? You’ll probably need a DBA. Luckily, Bizee can help.

[FILE ASSUMED BUSINESS NAME FILE ASSUMED BUSINESS NAME](https://orders.bizee.com/fictitious-business-name)

  ![File Dba Hero](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtaGVyby53ZWJw/file-dba-hero.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

  ![File Dba Hero](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtaGVyby53ZWJw/file-dba-hero.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Who Needs a DBA?
----------------

If you’re a sole proprietorship or partnership, you’ll likely need a DBA. That’s because you’re unincorporated, so you didn’t file entity formation papers or choose a business name. Your legal name will be your business name unless you file a DBA.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

   ![Who Needs A Dba 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvd2hvLW5lZWRzLWEtZGJhLTEud2VicA/who-needs-a-dba-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Who Needs A Dba 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvd2hvLW5lZWRzLWEtZGJhLTIud2VicA/who-needs-a-dba-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)   ![Who Needs A Dba 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvd2hvLW5lZWRzLWEtZGJhLTMud2VicA/who-needs-a-dba-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Why File DBA?

   ![Why File Dba Info Mobile](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvd2h5LWZpbGUtZGJhLWluZm8tbW9iaWxlLndlYnA/why-file-dba-info-mobile.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Why File Dba Info](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvd2h5LWZpbGUtZGJhLWluZm8ud2VicA/why-file-dba-info.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Why File DBA?

1

Location-Specific Branding

A DBA lets each business location use a unique name under the same entity.

2

Privacy

When you form a business, it defaults to your name unless you register as an entity. (LLC, Corporation, Non-Profit)

3

Product Flexibility

Running multiple businesses? Use DBAs to clarify each service and stand out to clients.

4

Streamlined Rebranding

If your LLC name no longer fits your brand, a DBA lets you update your identity and better connect with your audience.

How to File a DBA
-----------------

   ![How To File A Dba 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMS53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![How To File A Dba 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMi53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)   ![How To File A Dba 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMy53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)   ![How To File A Dba 4](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtNC53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-4.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)   ![How To File A Dba 5](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtNS53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-5.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Find Which Entity Controls Business Formation

This is usually the Secretary of State, but sometimes it’s at the county level. If so, register your DBA in each county you operate in.

  ![How To File A Dba 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMS53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Download, Fill Out and Send the Online Form

Visit the website’s DBA section. You may be able to file digitally, though some systems still require faxing or mailing.

  ![How To File A Dba 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMi53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Pay the Filing Fee

Filing fees vary by state and entity type.

  ![How To File A Dba 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtMy53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Ensure Your Business Name Is Protected

A DBA doesn’t protect your business name. Form an LLC or corporation to secure it, or trademark it for stronger protection.

  ![How To File A Dba 4](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtNC53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-4.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

File Your Taxes

Whether you have a DBA or not, you'll need to file taxes. How and when depends on your business structure.

  ![How To File A Dba 5](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaG93LXRvLWZpbGUtYS1kYmEtNS53ZWJw/how-to-file-a-dba-5.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Trademark vs. DBA — Can You Have One Without the Other?

Worried About the Costs of Trademark Registrations?

Trademark vs. DBA — Can You Have One Without the Other?

You have a lot to consider when [putting together your limited liability company](https://bizee.com/limited-liability-company)
. From assembling your team to establishing your mission, there’s a lot to be done before you finally reach launch day.

  
However, even in that flurry of activity, it’s vital not to overlook the importance of protecting your company’s assets. To that end, your company’s name is among the most integral elements in your long-term success.

  
Let’s explore a DBA vs. trademark and how they might work together.

   ![File Dba Toc 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTEud2VicA/file-dba-toc-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![File Dba Toc 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTEud2VicA/file-dba-toc-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

As the starting point of your brand, you’ll have to decide if you need to trademark your company name or if a simple DBA—“doing business as” or fictitious name — is enough.

What Is a Trademark?

Imagine going through all the trouble of devising the perfect name for your business. You’re excited and ready to make a difference. Then you realize that another company either already has the same name or has sprung up to capitalize on your business’s success. Without a [trademark for your business name](https://bizee.com/articles/trademark-business-name)
, you have little to no defense against any emerging claims.

  
A trademark ensures that you have legal ownership over elements integral to your company, such as its name, logo, or slogan. Look around. Examples of successful trademarks are everywhere. Think of company names and logos like Apple, McDonald's and Nike, or specific products like Jell-O, Post-it, ChapStick and Vaseline. They are all trademarked and protected, meaning only the company owning the trademark can use these names and benefit from the products.

  
Filing for trademark rights isn’t overly complicated, although the process of finding a name that 1) suits your business and 2) isn’t already claimed can take a while. Once you file a trademark, it is infinitely renewable and recognized nationwide.

  

Benefits of Having a Trademark

  
A [trademark can add value to your business](https://bizee.com/business-formation/trademark-registration)
. It also highlights company reliability and trustworthiness when it comes to offered products or services. Many of today’s trademarked company names and products have entered into common everyday use. Think of how many times you’ve asked for a Band-Aid every time you had a scrape or cut! Here are  
seven benefits of having a trademark.  
  

1.  **Offers brand protection**. Prevents others from using the same company or product name, logo or tagline. (Think of Budweiser's "King of Beers" catchphrase. That has a [trademark](https://www.uspto.gov/trademarks/basics/trademark-patent-copyright)
    !) This helps protect your brand and reputation, especially when others are trying to take advantage of your success.
2.  **Ensures exclusive rights**. The protection for a trademarked name is nationwide and begins as soon as the trademark takes effect. So even though your business is known only in Boston — for now — your trademark is protected in New York, Los Angeles and everywhere in between.
3.  **Can be a major asset**. Many companies use their trademark to sell franchises. A successfully trademarked business can also attract potential buyers and help increase selling value.
4.  **Bolsters a company’s business and reputation**. Promotes the business that you are in and the products that you are selling through name, logo, and slogan recognition. A trademarked name and logo also helps represent what a business stands for.
5.  **Use of registration mark**. A trademark allows you to use the ® symbol, adding to the validity of your product and acting as a deterrent against others who may want to steal your name or logo.
6.  **Shields against trademark infringement**. Having a trademark protects against others applying for a similar trademark. It also does not allow a competitor to infringe on a trademark by playing dumb and using the "I did not know” defense.
7.  **Protection under the law**. A trademark allows you to sue for damages. It also allows the [U.S. Customs and Border Protection](https://www.cbp.gov/travel/us-citizens/know-before-you-go/prohibited-and-restricted-items?_ga=2.208029716.786009874.1597983268-76736874.1593401993)
     to block imports that infringe on your trademark. For example, knockoffs from other countries.

What Is a DBA?

A [DBA name](https://bizee.com/articles/understanding-dba-doing-business-as)
 has less to do with legal protection than trademarks and should not be confused with the legal business entity of your company. In some cases, a sole proprietor will use a DBA to separate their business from their individual name, or a corporation may opt to conduct business with a DBA name rather than using their corporation’s legal registered name.

  
This distinction between your own or your organization’s legal name is truly the only major benefit of a DBA name over other options.

   ![File Dba Toc 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTIud2VicA/file-dba-toc-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![File Dba Toc 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTIud2VicA/file-dba-toc-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

While a DBA name certainly has its place (and may very well be ideal for your company), its usefulness as a marketing and brand development tool doesn’t include any larger legal protections for your company or its meticulously selected name.

Key Features of a DBA

  

1.  **Easy to set up**. The filing process is not as complicated or as costly as setting up as registering a trademark.
2.  **Avoids using your real name**. A DBA lets you create a catchy and memorable name for your business that’s different from your registered entity name. This, however, opens a business owner to the risk of other people or businesses using that same name or a variation of it.
3.  **Limited to a local market/area**. A DBA does not extend across the country and is primarily allowed in a limited area.
4.  **A DBA does not form a business entity**. Rather, it allows you to use a fictitious name for your business that differs from your actual name.
5.  **No protection from competitors**. You cannot copyright or trademark your “fictitious” name or alias. Unlike the protections afforded to trademarks, your business assets and personal assets are not protected if you just file for a DBA.

DBA vs. Trademark: How to Decide

So, we’ve laid out a basic description for both [trademark name](https://bizee.com/articles/file-trademark-on-your-own)
 and DBA name. Now, let’s take a look at some key ways in which these two types of names compare.

  
**Protection**. Legal trademark and DBA names are designed for very different functions. As described above, a DBA creates a buffer between a legal entity as the name you use to market and promote your company, whereas a trademark name is inextricably concerned with the distinction between your company and others with names or even missions like it. If you have both of these needs, then you can easily file both a DBA and a trademark name, as this is a common practice among businesses.

  
**Name ownership**. If you really want to secure exclusive rights to your company’s name — perhaps you’re thinking long-term branding and expansion, which is never a bad idea — then you certainly will want to trademark. DBA names don’t give you the right to claim anything about your business’s name, at least not across the board. In many cases, businesses in an area can “claim” duplicate DBA names. Trademarks, however, are all about ownership of your name and the elements therein.

  
**Legal rights**. Aside from how you use your business name and your interest in having exclusive rights, you’ll also need to fully understand the legal protections or lack thereof involved with each. Yes, we’ve covered, but as the primary difference between trademark and DBA names, it bears repeating. DBAs offer virtually no legal rights. You have the right to use a name for your company, not to defend it against the competition. Trademarks and DBAs can work together to provide the best of both worlds though.

  
**Cost**. One key reason you should decide whether you want to secure a trademark vs. DBA name for your business is the cost involved. While trademark names can run into hundreds of dollars, a DBA name bears an incredibly affordable price, sometimes as low as $50. It all depends on the level of trademark (state vs. federal, the latter of which costs significantly more) you’re seeking, and that’s not even considering the [potential need for legal assistance](https://bizee.com/articles/contact-a-lawyer-to-trademark-search)
.

   ![File Dba Toc 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTMud2VicA/file-dba-toc-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![File Dba Toc 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZmlsZS1kYmEtdG9jLTMud2VicA/file-dba-toc-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

One key reason you should decide whether you want to secure a trademark vs. DBA name for your business is the cost involved.

Can You Trademark a DBA?

If you want to use a DBA for a particular product or service, you can trademark your DBA, giving it the same legal protections provided to trademarked companies and brands.

  
By having a [trademark for your DBA](https://bizee.com/articles/trademark-vs-dba-can-you-have-one-without-the-other)
, you gain all the benefits and protections of having a registered trademark. It keeps the competition from stealing your trade name or any similar sounding name and can also contribute to your unique brand identity.

Getting Trademark or DBA Help with Bizee

Getting a better understanding of how a trademark and a DBA function within your business can help you make wiser decisions for your company’s future. We also understand how overwhelming it can be to build a new company from the ground up. That’s why we make it our business to give you the best possible launchpad for your latest venture.

  
At Bizee, we give entrepreneurs like you the tools to maximize your impact on the market. Our Trademark and DBA filing services can take care of all the details for you, allowing you to focus on forming and growing your business.

--------------------------

   ![Info Corporate Llc Kit 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaW5mby1jb3Jwb3JhdGUtbGxjLWtpdC0xLndlYnA/info-corporate-llc-kit-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Info Corporate Llc Kit 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaW5mby1jb3Jwb3JhdGUtbGxjLWtpdC0yLndlYnA/info-corporate-llc-kit-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

Starting and Managing a Business Involves a Lot of Paperwork

When you run your own business, there are so many things to do that paperwork often gets pushed down to the bottom of the to-do list. But as a business owner, you're legally obliged to keep complete and accurate records. Your records must contain formation paperwork, shareholder information, resolutions, meeting minutes and licenses, as well as other important and formal documents. It's vital to keep these documents safe and well organized to avoid risking legal problems, fines or compliance issues.

  ![Info Corporate Llc Kit 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvaW5mby1jb3Jwb3JhdGUtbGxjLWtpdC0xLndlYnA/info-corporate-llc-kit-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

A short, fitting, and distinctive name Bizee's LLC corporate kit is made up of a binder of forms, certificates, papers and other items beautifully produced and personalized for your business demonstrates confidence, defines your business, and generates buzz. It is the foundation for your entire brand.

Form My LLC


---------------

Entrepreneurship is booming, and we're proud to be one of America's fastest-growing companies. Here's how you can start your LLC in six straightforward steps:

*   1
    
    Name Your LLC
    
    Your business name is the first impression you make. It's essential to pick a name that stands out and accurately represents your brand. In addition to selecting a unique name, you'll need to include a designator like "LLC" or "Limited Company" to indicate your business structure.  
      
    Tips:  
      
    
    1\. Ensure your name is distinctive to avoid legal issues.
    
    2\. Check your state's specific naming requirements.
    
    4\. Use our [Business Name Search](https://bizee.com/form/business-name-search)
     tool to check the availability in your state.
    
    5\. Not settled on a business name yet, our [Name Generator](https://bizee.com/business-name-generator)
     can help.
    
*   2
    
    Provide an Address
    
    Your LLC needs an official business address. This could be your home address if you're running a home-based business, a rented office space, or even a [virtual address](https://bizee.com/form/virtual-mailbox)
    . Remember to check your state's regulations, as some states do not accept P.O. Box addresses.  
      
    **Pro Tip:** A virtual address can provide privacy and the flexibility to manage your mail from anywhere. Check out our [Virtual Address Service](https://bizee.com/form/virtual-mailbox)
     for a reliable solution.
    
*   3
    
    Assign a Registered Agent
    
    A registered agent is your legal point of contact with the state. They receive important documents and ensure your business complies with state regulations. While you can act as your own registered agent, we recommend using a [professional service](https://bizee.com/form/manage-your-company/registered-agent)
     to avoid the hassle and maintain privacy.  
      
    **Why Choose Us?**  
      
    With any of our business formation packages, you get one year of registered agent service for free. Let us handle the details so you can focus on growing your business.
    
*   4
    
    Provide Names and Addresses of LLC Members
    
    You'll need to submit the names and addresses of all your LLC members to the state. This step is straightforward but crucial for maintaining transparency and compliance.  
      
    **Note:** You can use street addresses or P.O. boxes for your LLC members' addresses, depending on your state's requirements.
    
*   5
    
    State the Purpose of Your LLC
    
    When filing your LLC, you must state the purpose of your business. This can be a specific description or a broad statement like "any lawful purpose." If you're still refining your business idea, a general statement will suffice and gives you the flexibility to expand later.  
      
    **Quick Tip:** Keeping it simple with "any lawful purpose" covers most business activities and can save time during the filing process.
    
*   6
    
    File the Articles of Organization
    
    The final step is to file your Articles of Organization with the state and pay the associated fees. This document officially creates your LLC. Filing can be done online or by mail, depending on your state.  
      
    **With Bizee, It's Easier:**  
      
    We handle all the paperwork and filing for you, ensuring everything is done correctly and efficiently. Save time and reduce stress by letting us take care of this crucial step.
    

Benefits of Forming an LLC
--------------------------

Choosing an LLC structure offers numerous advantages:

  ![Benefits Of Forming An Llc 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYmVuZWZpdHMtb2YtZm9ybWluZy1hbi1sbGMtMS53ZWJw/benefits-of-forming-an-llc-1.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

### 

Liability Protection

Safeguard your personal assets from business liabilities.

  ![Benefits Of Forming An Llc 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYmVuZWZpdHMtb2YtZm9ybWluZy1hbi1sbGMtMi53ZWJw/benefits-of-forming-an-llc-2.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

### 

Simplified Compliance

Enjoy fewer regulations compared to other business types.

  ![Benefits Of Forming An Llc 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYmVuZWZpdHMtb2YtZm9ybWluZy1hbi1sbGMtMy53ZWJw/benefits-of-forming-an-llc-3.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

### 

Tax Flexibility

Benefit from pass-through taxation, reporting business income on your personal tax return.

  ![Benefits Of Forming An Llc 4](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYmVuZWZpdHMtb2YtZm9ybWluZy1hbi1sbGMtNC53ZWJw/benefits-of-forming-an-llc-4.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

### 

Ease of Management

Manage your business with less formalities than a corporation.

Preparing For The Future

LLC Compliance Requirements


===============================

Staying compliant with state regulations is essential for the ongoing success of your LLC. This includes filing periodic reports, paying annual fees, and meeting tax obligations. View Your [State Specific Compliance Requirements.](https://bizee.com/business-filing-deadlines)

FAQs About Naming Your LLC in California

General Rules for LLC Names

These rules usually apply to all LLCs, regardless of the state they're formed in.

*   1
    
    Your LLC Name Must Be Unique
    
    The business name you select cannot be in use by any other corporation or LLC in the state. This is why it's so important to perform a CA Secretary of State business search before you begin your formation paperwork.
    
*   2
    
    Your LLC Name Must Not Be Confusable with Another Business Name
    
    It’s not enough for your LLC name to be unique. It also cannot be similar to the name of another LLC or corporation in the state. Furthermore, you cannot use any of the following features for differentiation:  
      
    
    *   Suffixes, such as Corporation, Company, Incorporated, Incorporation, Limited, Corp., Co., Inc., Ltd., LLC, etc.
    *   Definite articles, such as “A,” “An,” or “The”
    *   The conjunction "And," or “&"
    *   The singular, plural or possessive forms of words
    *   Abbreviations, punctuation, symbols, fonts, typefaces, etc.
    
*   3
    
    Your LLC Name Must Contain Certain Words
    
    All LLCs must use one of the following in their names, usually at the end of the name: “Limited Liability Company,” “L.L.C.” or “LLC.”
    
*   4
    
    Your LLC Name May Be Subject to Other General Restrictions
    
    Most states will not allow you to form LLCs with names that:  
      
    
    *   Are similar to the name of a federal or state agency or organization (e.g., FBI, FDA, Florida Department of Economic Opportunity, Florida Department of Revenue, Treasury, etc.)
    *   Suggest affiliation with a federal or state agency or organization
    *   Use the term “Olympic” or any terms that are trademarks of the International Olympic Committee
    *   Imply a purpose that would be illegal for your business to carry out
    

Specific Rules fo California Business Names

In addition to the general rules listed above, you'll need to follow California LLC law applicable to naming your business. For example, per California Code of Regulations Title 2, Division 7, Chapter 8.5, §21005, you may not choose a business name that is likely to mislead the public.

  
For example:

  
a. If the proposed name creates a false implication of government affiliation.

1.  A proposed name may imply a government affiliation if the proposed name contains the recognized name or abbreviation of a city, county, state, country, region or recognized subdivision within a state or country and/or includes a word or words that commonly denote governmental organization or authority.
2.  Words that commonly denote governmental organization include, but are not limited to, “Agency,” “Commission,” “Department,” “Bureau,” “Division,” “Municipal” or “Board.”

[![Arrow Right](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/icons/arrow-right.svg)](https://bpd.cdn.sos.ca.gov/be/forms/name-guidelines-restrictions-2022.pdf)

The Art of Naming Your Business

Finding the perfect business name can be tough. We have a complete guide to help you choose the right business name, but basically, you'll want a name that will:

*   Appeal to your customers
*   Be memorable enough to stand out
*   Best represent your product or services
*   Not be used by another business

[![Arrow Right](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/icons/arrow-right.svg)](https://bizee.com/articles/business-formation/guide-to-naming-your-business)

Need help coming up with business name ideas? Try our free name generator.

California Business Entity Search

Once you've decided upon a name, you'll want to perform a California business search to make sure it isn’t already taken by another business in the state.

  
You can use the state's [online portal](https://bizfileonline.sos.ca.gov/search)
 to do a name search. Or you can use our simple and convenient Business Name Search tool, which will search the California Secretary of State registry for you.

 name doesn't infringe on the trademark or service mark of another business. The easiest way to ensure you're in the clear is to perform a trademark search through . If the trademark isn't already in use, you can even register it yourself.

DBA in California

You can do business under a name different from your legal LLC name. California calls this a fictitious name, though you may be familiar with terms other states use, such as trade name, assumed name or "doing business as" (DBA). You may decide to use a fictitious business name in California for a variety of reasons.

  
For example, your primary business might be called California Leisure and Travel, LLC, and you have a chain called Hollywood Bus Tours. You could register an assumed name just for that brand. You'd do that by filing with the [clerk of the county](https://www.counties.org/counties)
 where your business is located. You can also have Bizee do it on your behalf through our DBA service.

  
Note: A trade name is not the same as a trademark. Learn more about [trademark vs. DBA](https://bizee.com/articles/trademark-vs-dba-can-you-have-one-without-the-other)
.

**Register and Manage a Fictitious Name or DBA Name Through Our Easy-To-Use Service**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://bizee.com/business-formation/dba)

  ![Dba](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZGJhLnBuZw/dba.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

Register Your Business Name

You’ve performed a California Secretary of State business search, checked availability, followed the naming rules and determined whether you need a fictitious name. Now you can register your LLC name in one of two ways.

1.  If you don’t want to form your LLC right away, you can reserve the business name. You'll do this by completing a [Name Reservation Request](https://bpd.cdn.sos.ca.gov/corp/pdf/name-reservation-request-form.pdf)
     and filing it with the CA SOS. The name will be reserved for 60 days. You don't need to reserve a name if you're forming your business right away.
2.  If you’re ready to start your LLC, you can indicate your chosen business name when you file your Certificate of Formation with the CA SOS. Or you can have Bizee do it for you.

FAQs About Naming Your LLC in California

*   1
    
    Your LLC Name Must Be Unique
    
    The business name you select cannot be in use by any other corporation or LLC in the state. This is why it's so important to perform a CA Secretary of State business search before you begin your formation paperwork.
    
*   2
    
    Are There Any Rules for Naming My LLC in California?
    
    Yes. Most LLCs will be bound by general rules (applicable to all LLCs) and specific rules (applicable in the state of California). We’ve detailed these rules
    
*   3
    
    Can I Do Business Under a Different Name Than My Official LLC Name?
    
    Yes. You can conduct business under an assumed name. Details are [above](https://bizee.com/california-llc/california-business-names)
    
*   4
    
    Can I Reserve a Name for My LLC in California?
    
    Yes. The CA SOS allows you to reserve a name if you're not ready to start your business right away. Details are [above](https://bizee.com/california-llc/california-business-names)
    . If you're ready to start your business now, you don't need to reserve a name.

**Still Learning about Virtual Addresses?**

**What it is:**

A real street address with a unique suite number where your mail gets received, scanned, and uploaded to your virtual mailbox. You can view everything online. We hold the physical mail for 1–2 weeks, then securely shred it.

**What a virtual address isn’t:**

It’s not a PO Box or a physical address you can visit. It’s also not for accepting packages.

Benefits Of Virtual Address

Why Use a Virtual Address?
--------------------------

There are endless ways to use it, depending on who you are and how you work. But at its core, Bizee’s Virtual Address service comes down to two main features each with plenty of flexibility built in.

**Key Benefits**

![Pin Outline](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/icons/pin_outline.svg)

A physical street address where you don’t live or work:

**Credibility**

Boost credibility with a real U.S. street address at a premium, professional location.

**Privacy**

Keep your home address off the internet and out of the public record.

**Compliance**

Many states require a physical address to form. With Bizee, you can meet this requirement using a Business Virtual Address.

![Email](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/icons/email.svg)

Mail handling with digital scans and recordkeeping:

**Remote Access**

View and organize your mail from anywhere.

**Never Lose a Document Again**

Have a digital record of all your mail, ready whenever you need it.

**Save Time and Headaches**

Let us open, scan, upload and shred your mail.

![Hugeicons Package Remove](https://fls-9e98adad-e144-4ff5-b4ac-e9717504d40a.laravel.cloud/hugeicons_package-remove.svg)

|No Packages| Accepted

Please note that our virtual address service is designed to handle only letters and large envelopes.

Frequently Asked Questions


------------------------------

*   1
    
    I’m a self-employed contractor who wants a virtual address for my freelance business. Which do I use?
    
    You’ll use our Personal Virtual Address and should have no problem as long as the mail arrives in your name. As a sole proprietor doing business in their own name, there’s no real difference between your personal activity and that of your contract business.
    
*   2
    
    I’m a sole proprietor using a fictitious business name. How do I use your Virtual Address?
    
    Here, too, you can use our Personal Virtual Address, but unfortunately, you must use your legal name, not your DBA. As a sole proprietor, you can receive mail related to your business. However, the mail must still be addressed to you personally to qualify as personal mail.
    
*   3
    
    What happens if the sender misspells my name or the name of my business?
    
    That’s no problem, as long as they include the suite number and the name is close to the name on the account. This is why it’s crucial for the sender to include the suite number in case we have duplicate names in our system. We also accept common nicknames—Nick for Nicholas—but not a different name altogether.
    
*   4
    
    What if my company name and brand is the same as my personal name?
    
    You still need to decide whether the virtual address will be used for your company or for your personal use. Martha Stewart and Martha Stewart, Inc. (short for Martha Stewart Living Omnimedia, Inc.) are separate legal entities and treated differently in a range of legal and regulatory contexts including virtual addresses. You’ll even notice on the [USPS authorization form](https://about.usps.com/forms/ps1583.pdf)
     that it asks if the service is for business or personal use.
    
*   5
    
    What if I want to use a Virtual Address in multiple states?
    
    Yes, we can do this. It’s another case of needing to sign up for Bizee’s Virtual Address service in each state where you want an address and digital mailbox. Indeed, while our online system is fully secure, it’s also customized with a user-friendly experience. Get your mail quickly and reliably without feeling like you have to learn a completely new app.

Smarter Way  
To Manage Your Mail?

Choose your virtual address in minutes. Start receiving mail like a pro.

Sole Proprietorships with No Employees

If you're a sole proprietor with no employees,  
an EIN may not be needed.

  ![Need A Federal Ein 1](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbmVlZC1hLWZlZGVyYWwtZWluLTEucG5n/need-a-federal-ein-1.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

Single-Member LLCs

Single-member LLCs may use a Social Security Number.

  ![Need A Federal Ein 2](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbmVlZC1hLWZlZGVyYWwtZWluLTIucG5n/need-a-federal-ein-2.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

EIN Advantages

An EIN simplifies taxes and separates finances.

  ![Need A Federal Ein 3](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbmVlZC1hLWZlZGVyYWwtZWluLTMucG5n/need-a-federal-ein-3.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

EIN as Tax ID

An EIN acts as a tax ID for LLCs and other entities, simplifying tax reporting and establishing legal identity.

  ![Need A Federal Ein 4](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvbmVlZC1hLWZlZGVyYWwtZWluLTQucG5n/need-a-federal-ein-4.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

Using an EIN

   ![Using An Ein Info Mobile](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvdXNpbmctYW4tZWluLWluZm8tbW9iaWxlLnBuZw/using-an-ein-info-mobile.png?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Using An Ein Info](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvdXNpbmctYW4tZWluLWluZm8ucG5n/using-an-ein-info.png?p=lg&fm=webp)

Using an EIN

1

Tax Forms

Required for filing business tax returns and W9 forms.

2

Payroll Management

Use your EIN for forms related to managing employee payroll.

3

Business Bank Account

An EIN is necessary to set up a business bank account.

4

Business Loans

You’ll need an EIN to apply for business loans.

Frequently Asked Questions

Establish Your Business With an EIN

Do I Need an EIN for my LLC? (Plus Other Important FAQs)

You've done all the legwork to form your business, but you're still left wondering, “Do I need an Employer Identification Number (EIN) for my LLC?” The short answer is that you might. An EIN is a nine-digit federal tax identification number used by the Internal Revenue Service (IRS) to identify business entities.

  
In this guide, you'll learn whether or not your LLC needs an EIN and why it would be beneficial to secure one, even if it’s not mandated. Got questions? This guide covers all the FAQs so you don't miss a thing.

What Is an EIN? Is It the Same as an LLC?

An EIN is not the same as an LLC (Limited Liability Company).

  
An EIN, also known as a federal identification number or business tax ID, is a tax identity. The IRS assigns EINs to distinguish unique business entities, including sole proprietors, LLCs, corporations, partnerships, and nonprofit organizations.

  
[What is an LLC?](https://bizee.com/limited-liability-company)
 An LLC is a type of legal business entity created by state statutes. It's the fastest and easiest legal structure for your business to adopt. An LLC provides legal coverage of assets and liabilities as well as pass-through taxation.

  
The IRS doesn't require most sole proprietorships or single-member LLCs to have EINs. However, there may be some scenarios where your LLC is obligated to secure an EIN, so let's dig deeper.

If I Have an LLC, Do I Need an EIN?

If you have an LLC, you might need an EIN. Your LLC will require an EIN if any of the following scenarios apply:  
  

*   You have or are planning to hire employees.
*   You're operating a multi-member LLC.
*   You're a single-member LLC and want to be taxed as an S Corp or corporation.
*   You pay employment, alcohol, excise, tobacco, or firearms taxes.
*   You have a [Keogh plan](https://www.irs.gov/retirement-plans/retirement-plans-for-self-employed-people#:~:text=What%2527s%2520a%2520Keogh%2520plan%253F)
    .
*   You do business with trusts, nonprofit organizations, estates, real estate mortgage investments, plan administrators, and farmers’ cooperatives.
*   You took ownership of an existing LLC.
*   You wish to restructure as a corporation.

  
For more detailed information, visit the IRS website, or hire a tax or startup business consultant to guide you. Now, let's take a look at the benefits of having an EIN.

   ![Tax Breaks Credits Security Options](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvdGF4LWJyZWFrcy1jcmVkaXRzLXNlY3VyaXR5LW9wdGlvbnMud2VicA/tax-breaks-credits-security-options.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Tax Breaks Credits Security Options](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvdGF4LWJyZWFrcy1jcmVkaXRzLXNlY3VyaXR5LW9wdGlvbnMud2VicA/tax-breaks-credits-security-options.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

There are several business-related benefits of having an EIN for your LLC.

Benefits of Having an EIN

There are several business-related benefits of having an EIN for your LLC. Let's say you're running a new LLC and have no intention of hiring employees or setting up a retirement plan; therefore, you don't need an EIN. But should you get one? The answer is a resounding yes. An EIN does much more than just serve as a business tax identifier.

  
Even if obtaining an EIN is not mandated for you by the IRS, there are many benefits of getting an EIN for your LLC:  
  

*   Create a clear distinction between your business and yourself
*   Make it easier to secure startup funding
*   Enable yourself to open a business bank account
*   Establish business credit
*   Get assistance with bookkeeping and tracking of business finances
*   Add an additional layer of security and privacy to your business
*   Protect yourself from identity theft
*   Build professional credibility with vendors and customers
*   Speed up the process of attaining business licenses and permits
*   Receive tax breaks and credits for business expenses, salaries, and wages

  
To minimize business costs and save time, we suggest getting an EIN sooner rather than later.

Is an EIN the Same as an SSN for an LLC?

The main [difference between a Social Security number (SSN) and an EIN](https://bizee.com/blog/post/ein-vs-ssn-whats-the-difference)
 is that an SSN is for individuals, while an EIN is for businesses. The IRS tracks your business’s filings using an EIN. Many small business owners find it helpful to think of an EIN as an SSN for their business.

  

Should I Use an SSN or an EIN for Taxes?

  
If you do not have staff, a self-retirement plan, or excise tax payments, and you are a sole proprietor or single-member LLC, your SSN can be used for tax filing.

  
However, there are some compelling reasons for filing taxes using an EIN as opposed to an SSN. An EIN will do the following:

  
Provide more privacy and security as your SSN number won't be on public documents  
Enable you to file business taxes separately and establish a business history  
Give you the flexibility to hire employees and secure funding without any delay

   ![Ein Privacy Security Taxes](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZWluLXByaXZhY3ktc2VjdXJpdHktdGF4ZXMud2VicA/ein-privacy-security-taxes.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Ein Privacy Security Taxes](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZWluLXByaXZhY3ktc2VjdXJpdHktdGF4ZXMud2VicA/ein-privacy-security-taxes.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

The main difference between a Social Security number (SSN) and an EIN is that an SSN is for individuals, while an EIN is for businesses.

What Do I Need to Get an EIN for My LLC?

In order to obtain a new EIN, an SS-4 application form is required. To complete this application without any issues, you must have the following information available:  
  

1.  **Your business’s legal name and official address**: Enter the legal name used on your formation documents. If you're operating under a [“Doing Business As” DBA](https://bizee.com/blog/post/understanding-dba-doing-business-as)
    , use that name on the application, and add your official business address. Virtual addresses are accepted.
2.  **Type of legal entity**: Are you a sole proprietor, LLC, nonprofit organization, or corporation?
3.  **Start date**: If you have already filed as an LLC, enter the date of formation. Otherwise, enter the date you intend to start your business.
4.  **Owner’s name and tax ID**: For domestic LLCs, you can use your SSN as a tax ID. For international LLCs and business owners who don’t have an SSN, use your appointed Individual Taxpayer Identification Number (ITIN).
5.  **Number of LLC members**: How many members are in your LLC?
6.  **Reason for applying for EIN**: Are you hiring employees, creating a pension plan, or changing entity types?
7.  **The maximum number of employees expected in the next 12 months**: Include an accurate prediction of your future hiring needs.
8.  **Will you pay employment taxes annually or quarterly?** Once you decide, be sure to tell the IRS immediately.

How to Apply for an EIN

You can apply for an EIN online, via fax or mail, or through Bizee’s EIN filing service.

  
To file directly with the IRS, complete the [online application form](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/small-businesses-self-employed/get-an-employer-identification-number)
 between Monday and Friday, 7 a.m. to 10 p.m. EST. The IRS issues the EIN upon submission and verification of the form — this usually just takes a few minutes. However, the online application is only available for LLCs with a domestic, U.S.-based address.

   ![Ein Application Comparison Bizee Irs](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZWluLWFwcGxpY2F0aW9uLWNvbXBhcmlzb24tYml6ZWUtaXJzLndlYnA/ein-application-comparison-bizee-irs.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Ein Application Comparison Bizee Irs](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvZWluLWFwcGxpY2F0aW9uLWNvbXBhcmlzb24tYml6ZWUtaXJzLndlYnA/ein-application-comparison-bizee-irs.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

You can apply for an EIN online, via fax or mail, or through Bizee’s EIN filing service.

To apply by fax, complete the SS-4 form and fax it to 855-641-6935. The fax line is open all seven days of the week, 24/7. Faxed EIN requests have a turnaround time of four business days.

  
Domestic LLCs can mail the hard copy of form SS-4 to the following address:

  
Internal Revenue Service Attn: EIN Operation Cincinnati, OH 45999

  
The processing time for mailed applications ranges between four to five weeks.

  
LLC owners with international addresses and no legal U.S. address or a responsible party that can file on their behalf need to call 267-941-1099 between 6 a.m. and 11 p.m. EST, Monday through Friday, to get their EIN.

What to Do After Getting an EIN

Your EIN is active and ready as soon as you receive it from the IRS. Use it to open a dedicated business bank account, secure funding, or hire employees.

Will I Ever Need to Change My EIN?

Yes, there might be cases where you'll need to change your EIN. If you're changing ownership or the type of business structure you operate, you will need to apply for a new EIN.

  
Here are a few scenarios that require changing your EIN:  
  

*   You already got an EIN as a sole proprietor and now you are incorporating.
*   You are currently registered as a single-member LLC and wish to restructure to a multi-member LLC or corporation.
*   You have an LLC EIN and elect to [file LLC taxes as an S Corp](https://bizee.com/blog/post/s-corp-self-employment-taxes)
    .
*   You add new partners to an existing LLC.

  
Changing your business name or location does not require changing your EIN. A business formation service can help you understand whether or not your LLC needs a change of EIN.

Frequently Asked Questions

Does EIN Mean You Own a Business?

  
Yes, having an EIN means you own a business, as it's administered by the IRS to identify business entities for tax purposes. But keep in mind that acquiring an EIN as a sole proprietor does not make your business a legitimate business entity. To form a legal business entity that provides liability and assets protection, like an LLC or corporation, you must register your business with your Secretary of State.

  

Can I Look Up My EIN?

  
I don’t remember my EIN, where can I find it? Unfortunately, the IRS doesn’t provide an EIN directory service where you can use your business name or any other identifier to find your EIN.

  
However, you can look up your LLC’s EIN on previous tax forms, bank statements (if you used it to open a business bank account), or your original confirmation notice. If none of these are handy, call the IRS Business and Specialty Tax Line at 1-800-829-4933.

  
When you incorporate with Bizee, you can easily access your EIN and crucial business documents via your online dashboard.

  

Can I Close or Cancel My EIN?

  
Once assigned, the IRS doesn’t cancel EINs. However, you can write to the IRS and ask them to close the EIN account if you deem it unnecessary. You need to provide the legal entity name, address, and reason for closing the account.

Establish Your Business With an EIN

Obtaining an EIN is an excellent way to establish and grow your business. To obtain an EIN, you must form a legal business entity, which guarantees the safety of your business and its assets. Table of Contents

What Is a Business Permit?

Seven Common Types of Business Licenses and Permits

A Note on Federal Permits

Prepare Your Company for Success

What Is a Business License?

Think of a business license as your official permission slip from the state government authorizing you to operate in a specific location. It’s like a driver’s license for your business—a green light to conduct business legally. Before getting your license, you’ll need to demonstrate competency in your field and familiarity with relevant laws and regulations. Having a license verifies you’ve met the minimum operating requirements and can now focus on building your dream.

What Is a Business Permit?

A business permit, typically issued by a state or federal agency after an inspection, ensures your startup adheres to your industry’s safety and health standards. It certifies that your business operates according to industry benchmarks, safeguarding your employees, customers, and the public. A permit can also boost trust with potential clients and partners, signifying your legitimacy and commitment to following regulations.

What Licenses and Permits are Needed to Start a Business?

To ensure compliance with local and federal regulations, it’s crucial to thoroughly research and understand the specific licensing and permit requirements for your business structure and activities. The permits and licenses you need will depend on a unique blend of factors.

  

Industry

  
Regulations differ vastly across industries. A bakery needs a health department permit for safe food handling and inspections, while a software company likely won’t. Construction companies will need permits for various projects, while a freelance writer might not require any permits.

  

Location

  
Requirements vary by state, county, and even city. A business in Newark, New Jersey, may have local ordinances that are not required in [San Francisco, California](https://www.sf.gov/resource--2022--permits-and-licenses-business)
. Always check with your local government for the latest regulations.

  

Business Structure

  
Sole proprietorships might have fewer licensing hurdles than limited liability companies (LLCs) or corporations. Depending on your structure, you may need additional professional licenses for specific roles within your company, such as a contractor’s license for construction companies.

  

Business Activities

  
Beyond your core business activities, consider any additional services you provide. A bakery selling custom cakes might need an extra permit for decorating services, while a graphic designer creating logos for clients might need a business tax license.

   ![Business License Toc](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtbGljZW5zZS10b2Mud2VicA/business-license-toc.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)  ![Business License Toc](https://bizee.com/img/http/aHR0cHM6Ly9mbHMtOWU5OGFkYWQtZTE0NC00ZmY1LWI0YWMtZTk3MTc1MDRkNDBhLmxhcmF2ZWwuY2xvdWQvYnVzaW5lc3MtbGljZW5zZS10b2Mud2VicA/business-license-toc.webp?p=lg&fm=webp)

A data breach can weaken a starting enterprise, eroding trust, incurring hefty fines, and leading to legal trouble.

Seven Common Types of Business Licenses and Permits

The particular permits or licenses you need will vary depending on your location and industry. Some of the most commonly encountered licenses and permits for startups include:  
  

1.  **General business license**. This is often the first license obtained, authorizing basic business operations within a specific location.
2.  **Seller’s permit**. If you sell physical products, you’ll most likely need a seller’s permit, also known as a sales tax permit, to collect and pay sales tax.
3.  **Home occupation permit**. Working from home often requires a specific permit to ensure your residential activity complies with zoning regulations.
4.  **Business signage permit**. This allows you to display your business name and logo outside your place of business.
5.  **Zoning permits**. Depending on your location and business activity, you might need a zoning permit to ensure your operation complies with the designated land use.
6.  **Building permits**. Any construction or major renovations on your business premises will likely require a building permit.
7.  **Environmental permits**. Businesses that generate waste, discharge pollutants, or handle hazardous materials may need environmental permits from state or federal agencies.

  
Beyond these general licenses and permits, some industries have additional licensing requirements. For instance, [healthcare providers](https://telehealth.hhs.gov/licensure/getting-started-licensure)
, lawyers, and plumbers require specific professional licenses to practice. 

Licensing and Permitting Differences Between States

Business license and permit requirements [vary significantly from state to state](https://bizee.com/articles/how-to-get-a-business-license-in-all-50-states)
, impacting startups in specific industries. Here are some key areas where you might encounter differences:  
  

*   **Tech and e-commerce**. Startup-heavy industries like tech or e-commerce might have specific state-level requirements. For example, California has a [Data Brokers Registration Act](https://cppa.ca.gov/data_brokers/)
     requiring businesses that collect consumer data to register with the state Attorney General’s office, a regulation not present in all states.
*   **Licensed professionals**. Licensing requirements for certain professionals, such as engineers or financial advisors, might vary by state. Some states require certifications or registrations, while others don’t.
*   **Home-based businesses**. Regulations for home-based businesses can differ. Some states might have a more streamlined process for home office permits, while others have strict zoning restrictions impacting home businesses. To be sure your company has all the essential paperwork to operate, you should look into the licenses and permits that your state requires. Most states have a small business agency or chamber of commerce that offers state-specific information to entrepreneurs.

A Note on Federal Permits

While most businesses won’t need federal permits, [some industries operate](https://www.uschamber.com/co/start/startup/business-licenses-and-permit-guide)
 under the federal government’s watchful eye. These are typically heavily regulated sectors like:  
  

*   Broadcasting and transportation—think of radio stations that need FCC licenses or airlines that require Federal Aviation Administration (FAA) permits.
*   Manufacturing and distribution—if you’re making food, drugs, or medical devices, you might need a permit from the Food and Drug Administration (FDA).
*   Businesses with an environmental impact—businesses generating hazardous waste or handling specific materials may need permits from the Environmental Protection Agency (EPA).
*   Alcohol and tobacco—producing, importing, or distributing these products require a license from the Alcohol and Tobacco Tax and Trade Bureau (TTB). 
*   Farming and livestock—businesses involved in agriculture may need permits from the Department of Agriculture for certain activities. 

  
To avoid potential fines, penalties, or legal issues caused by operating without the proper documentation, it is critical to research, understand, and stay current on your industry's specific regulations and requirements, just as it is with state requirements. 

Prepare Your Company for Success

Recognizing the distinctions between business licenses and permits and determining which are required matters when starting a business. It assures that you comply with all local, state, and federal regulations. A proactive approach, which includes thoroughly researching essential paperwork and regulations, will help you avoid legal complications and heavy penalties while also laying a solid foundation for your company's future success.

Frequently Asked Questions


------------------------------

*   1
    
    Do I need an EIN if I already have an LLC?
    
    Yes — an EIN is required to hire employees, open business bank accounts, and file federal taxes.
    
*   2
    
    Can I use my home address instead of a virtual address?
    
    You can, but a virtual address protects your privacy and boosts credibility.
    
*   3
    
    What’s included in the business kit?
    
    It includes a personalized binder, company seal, and stock certificates — everything to organize your entity.
    
*   4
    
    What’s the difference between a DBA and an LLC?
    
    An LLC is a legal business structure. A DBA is simply another name your LLC can operate under.
    
*   5
    
    How long does it take to get a business license?
    
    Timelines vary by location and industry — we’ll research and guide you through it.

What is a |Virtual Address?|

Unlike a PO Box, a virtual address includes mail handling, digital scans, disposal services, and a virtual mailbox dashboard where all your mail is uploaded. Personal virtual address services must also comply with [Commercial Mail Receiving Agency requirements](https://about.usps.com/forms/ps1583a.pdf)
.

Who is it for?
--------------

A lot of people dream about traveling around the country—and the world—while taking their job with them and staying in touch with contacts back home. This can take a variety of forms including digital nomads, expats, and retirees living or traveling abroad.
